we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一次世界大戰的戰線到第二次世界大戰的馬吉尼線 , 然後我們進入冷戰、鐵幕、柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的論點是 , 與其建設安全 , 我們不需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲有名的橋 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是華麗亞河的橋 , 小說的主題是伊佛•安德里•安德里 , 它談到如何在歐洲和巴爾幹非常麻煩的部分 , 經過一段時間 , 歐洲和巴爾幹半島的建築 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫地團結在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我認為 , 同樣的 , 開放原始碼的安全 , 就是要把國際網路、國際網路、私人公共部門連結起來 , 並用策略性的溝通 , 大多是在社交網路上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物在各種方面受到攻擊 , 而沒有任何威脅的來源 , 都會被建築牆壁所解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	顯然 , 我是水手 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 線性 , 穿過印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它有音樂會沿著它的側側線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	那就是防止海盜攻擊 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜現在是世界上非常活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜也非常活躍於馬拉加海峽 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	它位於幾內亞海灣 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到它 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	它是全球交通運輸系統中的一萬億美元的不連續性 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 當時有20艘船 , 500名海軍陸戰隊持有宿主 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉移到不同類型的海洋 , 網路海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這裡有兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	此刻 , 他們被監禁了 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一張信用卡詐欺 , 用超過一百億美金 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 在全球經濟中 , 是2兆美元的連續性 。
two trillion a year .	一年兩兆美元 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這就在英國的國內生產總值之下 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以這個網路海 , 我們知道無止盡是基本的開放 , 也受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	在全球公有物中 , 我擔心的另一件事 , 是人口販賣、毒品、鴉片、歐洲從阿富汗到美國的威脅 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心來自安地斯山脊的古柯鹼 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運動 , 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣大部份在海上 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們這是一塊非常高科技的美國海軍艦隊 , 用來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是毒品卡特爾的半導員 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它是在南美的叢林建造的 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用低科技的火車抓住了它 , 它帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	第四個 , 精密的溝通 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣毒品、毒品、人、武器、神禁止大規模破壞的武器 , 是全球公有物威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	今天我們一起在阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一塊餅乾 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	全世界百分之八十到九十的盜版、鴉片和海洛因都來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	基地組織就在此處 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到其中一個非常強烈的暴動 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須解決的問題 。
so here we are , 21st century .	這裡是21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道20世紀的工具不會成功 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為 , 我們不會只從槍的桶子裡遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會只從槍的桶裡遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍隊的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這樣做時 , 我們必須做得很好 , 而且要有競爭力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放資源安全是關於國際、國際、私人公共的聯繫 , 由網路上的戰略通訊的概念結合在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子 , 說明這如何運作 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都是拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我想我讀到 , 人口統計學 , 二十、三十歲的年輕人 , 大部分都是在阿富汗的文盲 。 」
you would be correct .	你可能會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班長期在這些男人和女人都學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們在識字課程中讀書 , 和私營機構合作 , 和發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們教過超過二十萬阿富汗安全部隊來閱讀和寫作 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你在阿富汗讀書時 , 你通常會把一支筆放在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在儀式裡 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們用很大的驕傲的筆 , 把它放在口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這就把國際組織結合起來 , 有50個國家涉及到這個任務 , 這些發展機構 , 以及私人公共機構 , 來採取這種安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們戰鬥技巧 , 但我認為 , 開放原始碼安全意味著將更長久的安全聯繫起來 , 創造出更長壽的安全效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫做慈悲的姐妹船 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 舒適的 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的路易士 , 他們會做四十萬個病人的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它並不是由軍事組織所組成 , 而是由人道主義組織的結合:營運希望、微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織發送自願者 。
interagency physicians come out .	外科醫生出來了 。
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 帶著他的母親走了兩天 , 來到舒適的眼診 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被安排在極端的眼睛上時 , 他突然抬頭說: 「 媽媽 , 維歐•埃爾蒙諾 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽 , 我看到這個世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	乘以四十萬個病人的治療 , 這個私人的公開合作 , 和安全部隊合作 , 然後你開始用非常不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能從這張照片中挑出兩位美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這兩位年輕男孩兩邊的年輕男孩 。 這是一系列的棒球診所的一部分 , 我們在南加拉的宏大聯盟 , 國家的部門 , 設立這個部門 , 軍隊棒球員 , 他們是真正的軍人 , 但參與這個任務 , 他們在全美和加勒比海 , 在南部的宏都拉斯 , 創造了全美的保險 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它呈現給年輕男性和女性的典範 , 關於健身及生活的典範 , 讓我認為這能幫助我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	另一方面是災難性的災難 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍直升機 , 在2004年海嘯後參與 , 殺死了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中 , 2004年的海嘯 , 25 , 000人死於巴基斯坦的kamiri地震 , 2005 , 8萬人死了 , 海地地震大約有30萬人死了 , 更近期是日本地震的海嘯 , 以及它的核子產業 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際演員 , 國際關係 , 私人合作 , 和安全部門合作 , 帶來了這種災難 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些是開放資源安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它連接起來 , 越來越像這樣做 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	各位現在看到的是這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿富汗 , 這些必定是溝通的海道 , 或者這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 。 根據推特 , 這是世界的圖像 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特訊息 , 綠色是地理分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	它是大人口調查的完美驅動 , 世界上有六個大國在下降順序:中國、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要進入這些蚊帳 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談到阿拉伯之春 , 及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉另一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表了一場像這樣的演講 。 如同我對你們說的 , 我在facebook上 , 朋友我 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾大笑 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是用ap來執行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上有兩個地方被撿起來:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	頭條是:北約的需求需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百名來自印尼人和芬蘭人的朋友請求 , 大多是說: 「 我們聽說你需要朋友 , 順帶一提 , 哪些是nato ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是的 , 我們會笑 , 但這就是我們如何傳遞訊息 , 移動訊息是我們如何連結國際、國際、國際間、私人的 , 以及這些社交網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我介紹一下十一月 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛裡 。
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在阿富汗南部的頭盔 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我讓他來這裡提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、有能力的軍隊 , 他們能創造出真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們所在的核心 , 以及我們所做的事 , 來保護自由、言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的一切 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 生命並不是個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要軍隊 , 不論是戰鬥 , 或在戰場上 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我認為生命是個劇院 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須戴上它 , 正如我所想的 , 在21世紀 , 我們要如何創造安全 , 在真正的戰爭和危機中 , 將會有時候我們會用真正的力量 , 但現今我們談到的 , 軍隊可以成為21世紀的安全、國際的 , 私人的溝通聯繫 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我會說我們今天早些時候聽到維基百科 。 我常常用維基百科來查事實 , 就像你們所欣賞的 , 維基百科並不是由12位聰明的人鎖在一個房間寫文章 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天有數萬人輸入信息 , 每天有數百萬人接受這些信息 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對根本的觀點而言 , 沒有人像我們一起思考一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 我們沒有一個人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的視覺陳述非常簡單:一個每個人都可以自由地分享的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 透過結合國際、國際間、私人的、策略性的溝通 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常謝謝你們 。 謝謝 。
